<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">испари́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">isparítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-е́ние</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-énije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:испарение.html>испаре́ние</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">isparénije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:испарение.html>испаре́ния</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:испарение.html>испаре́ния</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:испарение.html>испаре́ний</a></b>)

***испариться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:испариться.html>испари́ться</a> (13077)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">испари́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">isparítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:испариться.html>испари́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">isparítʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:испаряться.html>испаря́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to evaporate, to vaporize, to turn into vapor</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to disappear, to vanish into thin air</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial<span class="ib-comma">,</span> by extension</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to walk; to be stolen</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">испари́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">isparítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">sense 3</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><span class="deprecated-label">plural</span><span class="ib-comma">,</span> past tense</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>бы́ли</a> вы́несенны</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">býli výnesenny</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:испаряться.html>испаря́ться</a> (21273)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">испаря́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">isparjátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:испаряться.html>испаря́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">isparjátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:испариться.html>испари́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to evaporate, to vaporize, to turn into vapor</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to disappear, to vanish into thin air</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">испаря́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">isparjátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">ис-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">is-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пачкать.html>па́чкать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">páčkatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:испачкать.html>испа́чкать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ispáčkatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пачкать.html>па́чкать</a></b>)

***испечь.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:испечь.html>испе́чь</a> (17212)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">ис-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">is-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:печь.html>печь</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pečʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:испечь.html>испе́чь</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ispéčʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:печь.html>печь</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to bake</li>
<li>to scorch <i>(said of the sun)</i></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:исписать.html>исписа́ть</a> (9363)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">ис-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">is-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:писать.html>писа́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pisátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:испить.html>испи́ть</a> (29456)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">ис-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">is-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пить.html>пить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:испить.html>испи́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ispítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">испива́ть</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to drink <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">a little, some of</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">+ genitive</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to drink up, to drink (all of something) <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">+ accusative</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively<span class="ib-comma">,</span> literary</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to drink in, to suffer (sorrow, loss, bitterness, etc.) <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">+ accusative</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:исповедовать.html>испове́довать</a> (17440)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">ис-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">is-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">пове́довать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">povédovatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:исповедовать.html>испове́довать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ispovédovatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr> or <abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><strong class="selflink"><a href = vnd.unilang:исповедовать.html>испове́довать</a></strong></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">испове́дать</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to confess, to hear the confession</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:исповедовать.html>испове́довать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ispovédovatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to profess <i>(faith, religion)</i>, to worship</li></ol>

***исподволь.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:исподволь.html>и́сподволь</a> (14446)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Per Vasmer, from earlier <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">и́сподоволь</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">íspodovolʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">ис-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">is-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:получать.html>по-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">po-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">дово́ль(<a href = vnd.unilang:но.html>но</a>)</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dovólʹ(no)</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:исподволь.html>и́сподволь</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">íspodvolʹ</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> little by little, gradually, by degrees</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:исполком.html>исполко́м</a> (12302)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:исполком.html>исполко́м</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ispolkóm</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:исполком.html>исполко́ма</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:исполком.html>исполко́мы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:исполком.html>исполко́мов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>executive committee<sup id="cite_ref-словопидия_1-0" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-словопидия-1"> | 1 | </a></sup>
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2011</b>,  Алишер Аминов (Alisher Aminov),  “Фурсенко <a href = vnd.unilang:претендовать.html>претенду́ет</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:членство.html>чле́нство</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:исполком.html>исполко́ме</a> УЕФА”, in <span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(Please provide the book title or journal name)</span> | <sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://www.alisheraminov.ru/publications/interviews/594/">[1]</a></sup>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:член.html>Член</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:исполком.html>исполко́ма</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:фифа.html>Фи́фа</a> Мутко <a href = vnd.unilang:должный.html>до́лжен</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:понимать.html>понима́ть</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:представлять.html>представля́ет</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:национальный.html>национа́льную</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:федерация.html>федера́цию</a>.</span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Člen <b>ispolkóma</b> FIFA Mutko dólžen ponimátʹ, što on predstavljájet nacionálʹnuju federáciju.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">The member of the Executive Committee of FIFA, Mutko, must understand that he represents the national federation.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>

***исполнительный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:исполнительный.html>исполни́тельный</a> (7122)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:исполнить.html>испо́лнить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ispólnitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-тельный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-telʹnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:исполнительный.html>исполни́тельный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ispolnítelʹnyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)исполни́тельнее</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)исполни́тельней</b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:самый.html>са́мый</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:исполнительный.html>исполни́тельный</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>conscientious <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">working thoroughly, executing orders precisely and fast</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li>executive <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">designed for execution</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:исполнительный.html>исполни́тельный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:директор.html>дире́ктор</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>ispolnítelʹnyj</b> diréktor</i> ― <span class="e-translation">executive director</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:исполнительный.html>исполни́тельная</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:власть.html>власть</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>ispolnítelʹnaja</b> vlastʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>executive</b> power, <b>executive</b> authority</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>obedient</li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">ис-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">is-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-по́лнить</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-pólnitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:исполнить.html>испо́лнить</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ispólnitʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:исполнять.html>исполня́ть</a></b>)

<li>to perform, to play</li>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:исполнить.html>испо́лнить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ispólnitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:исполниться.html>испо́лниться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ispólnitʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:исполняться.html>исполня́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to come true, to be fulfilled
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:исполниться.html>испо́лнилась</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:мой.html>моя́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:заветный.html>заве́тная</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мечта.html>мечта́</a>!</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Ispólnilasʹ</b> mojá zavétnaja mečtá!</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">My cherished dream has come true!</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">impersonal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to turn (of age)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>В</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:воскресенье.html>воскресе́нье</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>ему́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:исполниться.html>испо́лнилось</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:тридцать.html>три́дцать</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:год.html>лет</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">V voskresénʹje jemú <b>ispólnilosʹ</b> trídcatʹ let.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">He turned thirty on Sunday.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:исполнить.html>испо́лнить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ispólnitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>
